<div id="review_3507965594" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3507965594" />
    <a title="Woman Reading" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/101060033-woman-reading"><img alt="Woman Reading" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565479291p2/101060033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3507965594?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Woman Reading" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Woman Reading" href="/user/show/101060033-woman-reading">Woman Reading</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=3-stars-mildly-entertaining">3-stars-mildly-entertaining</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=read-women-2020-challenge">read-women-2020-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=fantasy-urban-fantasy">fantasy-urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3507965594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10149565466532512902"><b>3☆</b><br/><br/>Species tensions erupt in the supernatural world as extremist ghouls stoke hatred against vampires, their undead siblings. In this installment, ghosts on steroids <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Remnants  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> controlled by another paranormal figure of renown - voodoo Queen Marie Laveau - explode onto the scene. Will the powerful Marie be a friend or an enemy as she consolidates her power in New Orleans during the rising conflict?<br/><br/>Luckily for the vampires, Cat's friendship with Vlad (Dracula) bolster</span>
  <span id="freeText10149565466532512902" style="display:none"><b>3☆</b><br /><br />Species tensions erupt in the supernatural world as extremist ghouls stoke hatred against vampires, their undead siblings. In this installment, ghosts on steroids <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Remnants  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> controlled by another paranormal figure of renown - voodoo Queen Marie Laveau - explode onto the scene. Will the powerful Marie be a friend or an enemy as she consolidates her power in New Orleans during the rising conflict?<br /><br />Luckily for the vampires, Cat's friendship with Vlad (Dracula) bolsters the few vampire alliances. Vlad delivers some of the best scenes. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Much slower, I turned around to see Vlad examining his fingernails, as if his hands weren't still ablaze in the flames that had blasted the ghoul's head off moments before.<br />"What the hell was that?" I gasped.<br />"Premature inflammation," he replied. "Happens sometimes. Very embarrassing, I don't like to talk about it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br />And Cat has finally resolved her emotional issues by making her irreversible decision in the preceding book. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The image I'd had of myself as a child was someone I'd never be, and it was only recently that I realized it was okay to be who I was. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote> My main criticism with this series is how readily the main protagonists acquire super powers. This began with Bones in book #3, for Cat with book #4, and continues to accelerate with this book. Too easy.<br /><br />Here are links to my reviews for the rest of the series - <br /><br />#0.5 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3521352713" rel="nofollow noopener"><i>Reckoning</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#1 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3506778751" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>Halfway to the Grave</i> 2.5 ☆ </a><br />#2 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507883153" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>One Foot in the Grave</i> almost 3 ☆</a><br />#3 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507887440" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>At Grave's End</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#4 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507891054" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>Destined for an Early Grave</i> 3 ☆ </a><br />#6 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3508032167" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>One Grave at a Time</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#7 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3508102459" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>Up from the Grave</i> 3 ☆</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10149565466532512902" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_98195665" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/98195665" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/98195665?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10126658-this-side-of-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-hot-male-in-my-harem">hero-hot-male-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=faves-kings-of-the-harem">faves-kings-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=action-adventure">action-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=lover-the-cover">lover-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-romance">genre-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-jeaniene-frost">author-jeaniene-frost</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer98195665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4832878506193922993">Will Cat and Bones ever get any peace? The answer to that question seems to be a big resounding NO! Thank goodness! Without their ability to piss off everyone in a 100 mile radius I wouldn't be able to obsess over everything about this series! This book continues the vampire vs ghoul war that seems to brewing because of Cat's unusual abilities now that she has been turned in to a vampire. But she not only has the paranormal war to worry about, but her mothers recently forced vampirism and her Un</span>
  <span id="freeText4832878506193922993" style="display:none">Will Cat and Bones ever get any peace? The answer to that question seems to be a big resounding NO! Thank goodness! Without their ability to piss off everyone in a 100 mile radius I wouldn't be able to obsess over everything about this series! This book continues the vampire vs ghoul war that seems to brewing because of Cat's unusual abilities now that she has been turned in to a vampire. But she not only has the paranormal war to worry about, but her mothers recently forced vampirism and her Uncle Don's secret to contend with as well. <br /><br />This book was great, it delved more in to the world of vampire and ghoul politics and had all the characters come in from all the other books as well. I liked seeing Vlad and can not wait for his book to come out in the Night Huntress World spin off series. I also liked seeing Kira and Menchere's as well, and when Cat and Bone's caught, or rather heard them in the act it was fricking hilarious. <br /><br />That is another aspect I like about these books is the humour, at times they can be dark and bloody, but I love the touches of humour she adds as well. Not to say that there aren't a few poignant moments as well, the parts with Don made me cry like a baby and I thought it was very moving. <br /><br />Now as for Cat and Bones, the central characters, I love their connection and complete love and trust they have in eachother, which has really grown over the last four books. Cat has got to be one of my favourite heroines, she is funny, smart and can totally kick ass without being in-your-face irritating and over the top hardass. s for Bones, I am completely in love with him! <br /><br />And we may have another Chapter 32 situation in this book! Chapter 21 anyone?<br /><br />So another great installment in the series and I can not wait for more!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4832878506193922993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_123955808" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/123955808" />
    <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595947372p2/3108364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/123955808?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog">Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2011">books-read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-audio-books">read-audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2020">books-read-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer123955808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12924651936813108859"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>I was so excited to get this book, and start reading it as soon as it came out! I've been on Cat & Bones withdrawals because the 4th book in the series was a bit mehh, and then we got 2 books in the Night Huntress World spin-off, and I was not so happy with Spade's, and I did liked Mencheres.<br/><br/>But here we are back with Cat & Bones.... Ahhhh... Opening scene... LOVED IT! I wouldn't mind having him shackled to a cave wall! After that though it started going really slow for me.<br/><br/>The story was </span>
  <span id="freeText12924651936813108859" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />I was so excited to get this book, and start reading it as soon as it came out! I've been on Cat &amp; Bones withdrawals because the 4th book in the series was a bit mehh, and then we got 2 books in the Night Huntress World spin-off, and I was not so happy with Spade's, and I did liked Mencheres.<br /><br />But here we are back with Cat &amp; Bones.... Ahhhh... Opening scene... LOVED IT! I wouldn't mind having him shackled to a cave wall! After that though it started going really slow for me.<br /><br />The story was ok enough, but it wasn't GREAT. I had really high expectations for this book, and didn't feel like it met them 100%, even though it was a good book (I did rate it 4 stars!) I mainly feel like Cat lost some of her spark and spunk from the beginning of the series, and she didn't feel like she was as confident. And although she was funny at times, sometimes she got a little on my nerves. And that's not good since we're getting the story from her POV.<br /><br />Bones was amazing in this book however! OMG! I'm in love with him, he can do no wrong! His connection to Cat felt rekindled in this book where it was a bit lacking in the last NH book. And yeah, of course, that brings up the elephant in the room... Chapter 21!!!! I knew before hand from comments on GR to watch out for that chapter, so I paid extra attention, I might've read it twice ;) It was HOT, YOWZA, INTENSE and did I mention <i>REALLY HOT</i>? It has been compared to Chapter 32 of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2168860.One_Foot_in_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___2_" title="One Foot in the Grave (Night Huntress, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">One Foot in the Grave</a>, and I'll agree it gives it a run for the money. It all depends on your preferences. I actually went back and re-read Chapter 32 after finishing this book to be able to compare with a fresh image. There's a lot of biting involved in both, except OFITG was Bones doing the biting, in TSOTG was Cat. But biting aside, I think this book gives us a little bit more intense view of what else they were doing aside from all the biting ;) And I loved seeing Bones lose control! Enough said!<br /><br />One of my favorite lines in the book is from Bones, when he tells Timmy to ask what he wants about vampires but then he says <i>"If you ask me if I sparkle I'll kill you"</i> LMAO!<br /><br />Vlad... where do I start... He's the best! He had the best lines in the book (<i>"Premature inflammation! Very embarrassing, I don't like to talk about it!"</i> Come on! I was ROTFLMAO) There was plenty of him in this book and I still want more!<br /><br />Mencheres... 2 things.... 1 - Him having sex with Kira while Bones and Cat where waiting to see and could hear him... LOL 2 - The shorts and t-shirt at the airport?!?!? That I would have to see!<br /><br />Ian... Not enough of him in this one. I would love to see his character developed a bit more, I know he has to mature before he can get his own book but he has the potential. And I couldn't believe his comment about Veritas... I always picture her as a kid! Even though she's old as dirt.<br /><br />The twist at the end.... I could've used at least one more page after the last word!!!! WHAT?!?!?!?!? I'm dying to read the next book and see what the hell happened there!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12924651936813108859" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_163618782" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/163618782" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/163618782?book_show_action=true">Apr 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2011">2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer163618782" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7311556703708924451">If I'm honest, this book would have got 4 stars had I not read the other 4 installments in the Night Huntress series. The story, in my opinion, was quite weak and I can't find much to interest me in Marie's character. It's surprising actually because she's another quirky and unique member of Frost's creations, and I so adore all the others. Frost's true gift lies in creating wonderful and memorable characters, with no repetitions amongst them; by that I simply mean all of them are very different</span>
  <span id="freeText7311556703708924451" style="display:none">If I'm honest, this book would have got 4 stars had I not read the other 4 installments in the Night Huntress series. The story, in my opinion, was quite weak and I can't find much to interest me in Marie's character. It's surprising actually because she's another quirky and unique member of Frost's creations, and I so adore all the others. Frost's true gift lies in creating wonderful and memorable characters, with no repetitions amongst them; by that I simply mean all of them are very different, unlike Gena Showalter's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/476543" rel="nofollow noopener">Lords of the Underworld</a>, where I find that all of the Lords are different looking versions of the same character.<br /><br />For one, Cat is a heroine that I can relate to in so many ways (even now she has become a vampire). She's awesomely quirky and sarcastic, ruthless when she needs to be but compassionate as well. But then all the characters have distinctive traits, complete with their own sense of humour and extremely quotable lines (that I completely abuse on my blog). Even in this book, which didn't quite grab me as much as the previous ones, I cared all the way through what would happen to each and every one of them. It had so many varied elements that make a novel an instant favourite: humour, sadness, mystery, smut...<br /><br />I find it much more difficult writing reviews like this when I really enjoyed nearly every aspect of the book. I'm out of my comfort zone when I don't have whiny, so-called heroines to tear apart, or equally annoying brainless men who are used to try and sell a novel by repeatedly emphasising their looks and obvious lack of personality. Bones, on the other hand, is the most perfect and sexy kind of hero to have. I would start going on about his and Cat's awesome sex scenes again but people who read my reviews will start thinking that's all I talk about (hehe).<br /><br />However, Ms Frost, that cliffhanger was hardly necessary, was it? I was always going to read book number 6 when it comes out in August(!) without you being cruel and giving me something to tear my hair out about until then. It reminds me of Karen Marie Moning's ending to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6050298" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreamfever</a>, which was an even worse cliffhanger than this one. I nearly went crazy with the not knowing what the hell was happening until bloody <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7304203" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadowfever</a> was released. Some authors are sadists.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7311556703708924451" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_458421128" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458421128?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22018552-this-side-of-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2019">2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=own-digital-audiobook">own-digital-audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458421128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10065587067030416824">This review can also be found at <a href='https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I had fun with this re-read. It appears that I did like this one a little more the second time around since I only gave the book 3 stars when I read it in 2012. This isn't the best book in the series but I still found it enjoyable. I hadn't planned to listen to this book when I did but none of the audiobooks I started were working for me but everything seemed to work when I gave this one a try. I ended up listening to the entire audi</span>
  <span id="freeText10065587067030416824" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I had fun with this re-read. It appears that I did like this one a little more the second time around since I only gave the book 3 stars when I read it in 2012. This isn't the best book in the series but I still found it enjoyable. I hadn't planned to listen to this book when I did but none of the audiobooks I started were working for me but everything seemed to work when I gave this one a try. I ended up listening to the entire audiobook in just a couple of days and enjoyed my time back in the Night Huntress World.<br /><br />The last two books in the Night Huntress Universe focused on other couples so I was glad to see Cat and Bones back in the lead for this installment. Cat and Bones find themselves in the middle of a conflict between ghouls and vampires. They have to play their cards very carefully in order to get the outcome they hope to see. I really enjoyed seeing a little more in regards to Cat's developing powers and some of the more interesting side effects she encounters in this book. There are some other developments in this story that aren't easy for Cat to deal with.<br /><br />I love the characters in this series. Cat and Bones are always awesome and together they are amazing. I love the way Bones has no problem telling Cat what he feels and doesn't hesitate to do so. I also have a lot of love for the larger group. I loved getting to see Spade, Denise, Mencheres, and Kira play a part in this installment. Vlad was amazing in this book. I love his scenes with Cat even if he tends to steal a lot of her spotlight. I cannot wait to get to his books as I re-read this series.<br /><br />Tavia Gilbert does such a fantastic job with this series. I love all of the voices that she uses for the different characters but I think she might deserve some kind of award for the voice she uses for Bones. It is absolutely perfect. I think that one of the reasons that I enjoyed this book more than I did the first time I read it is her narration. She was able to bring this story to life in the most amazing way.<br /><br />I would recommend this series to others. While I don't think that this is the strongest book in the series, I had a good time with it and can't wait to read more books in this wonderfully crafted universe.<br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />I gave this book 3 stars back in 2012 and I am going to bump it up to 4 with this reading. This is not one of the stronger books in the series though. It felt like filler in some ways. I did think that learning more about Cat's abilities was pretty interesting and it was great to see this group of characters again. Vlad really seems to take the spotlight in any scenes that he is involved in and I just am loving his character more and more. Tava Gilbert did an amazing job with the narration once again.<br /><br />Book source: Audible purchase</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_138294414" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/138294414" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/138294414?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer138294414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9165392521278922670">I love how in this installment of the Night Huntress series, we have Bones and Cat happy.<br/><br/>It may sound cheesy, but there it is. In the last book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5604848.Destined_for_an_Early_Grave__Night_Huntress___4_' title='Destined for an Early Grave (Night Huntress, #4) by Jeaniene Frost' rel='nofollow noopener'>Destined for an Early Grave</a>, they were so far apart it hurt me to read it. While I love the tension of them at odds with each other, I hate how hard it is to read about what we know is a perfect-for-each-other-couple fighting.<br/><br/>In this book, they aren't fighting with each other. Bones' past isn't thrown in our faces, and they have a sweet and tender moment</span>
  <span id="freeText9165392521278922670" style="display:none">I love how in this installment of the Night Huntress series, we have Bones and Cat happy.<br /><br />It may sound cheesy, but there it is. In the last book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5604848.Destined_for_an_Early_Grave__Night_Huntress___4_" title="Destined for an Early Grave (Night Huntress, #4) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Destined for an Early Grave</a>, they were so far apart it hurt me to read it. While I love the tension of them at odds with each other, I hate how hard it is to read about what we know is a perfect-for-each-other-couple fighting.<br /><br />In this book, they aren't fighting with each other. Bones' past isn't thrown in our faces, and they have a sweet and tender moment where Cat breaks down the last wall she's held between them. There is, of course, the Big Bad. It's Apollyon, the leader of the ghouls. He is still trying to start a war between the vampires and the ghouls. He says that since Cat is a half-breed, even though she's pretty much a full-vampire now, she could still turn ghoul. So they need to kill her so she can't take over and rule all of the supernatural creatures. Right. It's kind of a big deal, since he's been trying to do so for ,oh 600 years or so. So killing Cat is nothing personal, right? Just business. <br /><br />But Cat is a bit more grown-up in this book. She doesn't make decisions without including Bones, and she doesn't run off half-cocked, and she doesn't do anything brash or foolish. I loved that. I have so wanted Cat to mature a bit more. Her mom has a *ahem* <i>new</i> role. I won't spoil it (Highland Hussy zips her lips). Tate has a couple of good scenes, and Don, oh Don, he has such an important role and I can't say one word about it without spoiling it! And it's not a small spoiler either!<br /><br />The breakout star of this book? Vlad. Without a doubt, I heart Vlad. My favorite line has been quoted everywhere, but it's worth the mentions. Cat is trying to convince Bones and Vlad to let a ghoul who'd tried to kill her go free as a gesture of goodwill. Suddenly the ghoul's head explodes.<br /><br /><i>"What the hell was that?” I gasped.<br />“Premature inflamulation,” he replied. “Happens sometimes. Very embarrassing, I don’t like to talk about it."</i><br /><br />The main reason I gave this book 4 rather than 5 flames is that Marie had such a huge role in both this book, and in the last book, and I don't know, I guess I was expecting...<b>more</b> from her. She has the potential and just wasn't utilized enough. She was the catalyst for some of the action, no doubt, and she was right there at the end, but I felt for as huge a role as Majestic is, she could have been in it more.<br /><br />Now onto the fun part...ch. 21. Ah, yes, I see you've heard of this? Yes, folks, ch. 21 is the new ch. 32. If you wear glasses, they will fog whilst reading ch. 21. I will say only one thing about it *hot candle wax* and I'll leave it at that.<br /><br />Oh, but one really huge giant tip?<br /><br />Read the Night Huntress World books <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6547187.First_Drop_of_Crimson__Night_Huntress_World___1_" title="First Drop of Crimson (Night Huntress World, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">First Drop of Crimson</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6871616.Eternal_Kiss_of_Darkness__Night_Huntress_World___2_" title="Eternal Kiss of Darkness (Night Huntress World, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Eternal Kiss of Darkness</a> first because this book WILL SPOIL THEM. I wish I'd known. I have them on my tbr list, but if I had known this I'd have made a point to read them last week . sigh.<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.com/2011/03/this-side-of-grave-by-jeaniene-frost.html">http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.co...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9165392521278922670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_134108946" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/134108946" />
    <a title="Lora" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4632071-lora"><img alt="Lora" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305237530p2/4632071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/134108946?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lora" href="/user/show/4632071-lora">Lora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">devoted fans of the series</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=pr-uf-crossbreed">pr-uf-crossbreed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer134108946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14228928920953078728">This truly saddens me. Each of the first four books in this series were astonishingly entertaining, and I had begun to wonder if Frost would ever deliver a book without it being wrapped in perfect packaging and tied with a gorgeous bow.<br/>Unfortunately, that time has come. While I figured Frost would have to hit a plateau eventually, I had hopes that that time would never come. Looks like <i>This Side of the Grave</i> is it. After being so pleased by the first four installments in this series, it is clear</span>
  <span id="freeText14228928920953078728" style="display:none">This truly saddens me. Each of the first four books in this series were astonishingly entertaining, and I had begun to wonder if Frost would ever deliver a book without it being wrapped in perfect packaging and tied with a gorgeous bow.<br />Unfortunately, that time has come. While I figured Frost would have to hit a plateau eventually, I had hopes that that time would never come. Looks like <i>This Side of the Grave</i> is it. After being so pleased by the first four installments in this series, it is clear why I'd have high expectations when starting the fifth installment. And while I <i>did</i> enjoy it, I don't think Frost came even close to her potential with this one.<br /><br />The plot is an obvious direction that most fans of this series have probably thought of before. With two equally powerful species coexisting for millennia, they're bound to clash at some point, right? Cat's abnormalities just happen to be the catalyst that sets it off, making hers and Bones's attempt at some peace and quiet be shoved to the back burner once again.<br />This idea of a species war could've been explosive and entertaining, but instead it mostly felt forced and anticlimactic. <br />Something about the plot (specifically, its execution) just felt off to me. THANKFULLY, Cat and Bones's chemistry is still there, and there are plenty of erotic and emotional moments between them that help to revive the story.<br /><br />Two words: Chapter. Twenty-One. If you're a fan of chapter thirty-two in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2168860.One_Foot_in_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___2_" title="One Foot in the Grave (Night Huntress, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">One Foot in the Grave</a>, you'll most likely enjoy chapter twenty-one in this. Think chapter thirty-two, only reversed, and with an extra splash of kink.<br /><br />I enjoyed getting to see the couples from the spin-off series (Mencheres and Kira, Spade and Denise) in their wedded bliss.<br />There is, as with all of Frost's novels, comedic relief. Bones wouldn't be Bones if he didn't make you crack up at least a few times. Although I <i>did</i> feel that there was far less of that in this installment than in the previous books.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I have to wonder if Ian will end up with Veritas, the Law Guardian who's as old as Mencheres. He makes a sexual comment about her towards the end, and while this <i>is</i> Ian we're talking about, it could happen. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Honestly, I feel like crap for having said anything even remotely cross about this book. I feel like I'm kicking a favorite pet here. But I have to give credit where credit is due, and I don't feel that Frost deserves as much credit with this one as she did with her previous novels.<br /><br />I'm crossing my fingers that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7954556.One_Grave_at_a_Time__Night_Huntress___6_" title="One Grave at a Time (Night Huntress, #6) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">One Grave at a Time</a> will bring back the magic of the first four books in this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14228928920953078728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer203716532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13669968700011912431">My review would be a broken record at this point. What can I say that I haven't mentioned already? I love the lore. I love Bones. I love the fierce action. I love Bones. I love the secondary characters especially Vlad. I love Bones. I love the steamy scenes. I love Bones. I love the relationship between Cat and Bones. I love Bones. See broken record.<br/><br/>One of my favorite paranormal series, but I must be clear... it's not a Young Adult book. Definitely not YA... </span>

          </span>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4ThGtKg8uALjKugW98PiPXrb8TZQ8WNr/tjhz6SCOsHbHi9mE2JxakQBXHcANujirIQW/p587Qylpqd+acHIWw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('E3f5b1O4GGS85rHX4YTndwLoTc4XFIcxHtSn/LmiqVApUZC96ObRDBvNBbYWce2o1LeqBtmZCVZFquFNdOFbyg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9111553377543456585">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText9111553377543456585" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
